	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'fc2a7a7129563fbc5037cf0613562e275c27c8b6') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '40ee2d1cab76b5f67c3e3629473d17bf62f9c573') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'fc2a7a7129563fbc5037cf0613562e275c27c8b6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '27ba4bfa444479d5128c2f29685e66b979a435d0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '27ba4bfa444479d5128c2f29685e66b979a435d0') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '513b82ea75fbb7687b63344f02498e5ac561da3b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '27ba4bfa444479d5128c2f29685e66b979a435d0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') != '58517499e8699b69d8a77c734e5cc114ccfd2ce5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== '58517499e8699b69d8a77c734e5cc114ccfd2ce5') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== '3a1ad4fe3d6ba254333d61a2d7ef502b7cd6db33') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== '58517499e8699b69d8a77c734e5cc114ccfd2ce5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/900_software_update/OIDplusPageAdminSoftwareUpdate.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();

}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') != '54a85b0dc665e35b6b3530888d3275ca41709453') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');

	}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != 'c4c8fc7d9402f8296d9342cf151798a415f9823e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'c4c8fc7d9402f8296d9342cf151798a415f9823e') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '8e76b1798f81d1147d29059b9c5fe26c9da89ab9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'c4c8fc7d9402f8296d9342cf151798a415f9823e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != 'a6ec02b6ab738c8aaf47e18efb440cbcc426d778') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'a6ec02b6ab738c8aaf47e18efb440cbcc426d778') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '34d566232f1ab732db86a6cb1726beaca804a369') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'a6ec02b6ab738c8aaf47e18efb440cbcc426d778') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}
